Thisn// ensures we don't break anyone's use of the element.nnfigure {n margin: 0;n}nnn// Imagesnnimg {n vertical-align: middle;n}nn// Responsive images (ensure images don't scale beyond their parents)n.img-responsive {n .img-responsive();n}nn// Rounded cornersn.img-rounded {n border-radius: @border-radius-large;n}nn// Image thumbnailsn//n// Heads up!
